Comparing Tranquility (Build: 3272045) to Singularity (Build: 3246005)

Want to be notified of new patches? Hop into #hoboleaks on Tweetfleet Slack! Instructions on how to join Tweetfleet Slack here.
Please note that Singularity will be kept inaccessible except for specific testing windows, and may fall significantly behind Tranquility in patches. The Tranquility/Singularity diff (homepage) may not be particularly useful for the time being. Refer to the latest Tranquility patches instead.

Find Hoboleaks useful and want to provide some support at no additional cost to yourself?
Use affiliate code HL (short for HoboLeaks) the next time you make a purchase through the official EVE store, which has Omega, PLEX, and much more. The small commission we receive helps Hoboleaks remain ad-free. Thank you! ♥

92183 - CONCORD-Carrier Rogue Analysis Beacon In response to the growing Rogue Drone outbreaks of YC128, CONCORD commissioned a Carrier specific version of the CONCORD Rogue Analysis Beacon (CRAB).

Unlike the original version, this one was able to mask drones and fighters from any incoming Rogue Drones. It also used a subtler, more thorough approach to signal analysis that resulted in less system interference.

NOTE: CRAB linking may not be possible if system signal interference is too high, or if the linking capsuleer has insufficient Complex Encryption Qubits (CEQ).

WARNING: Linking to this CRAB will render your ship immobile until the powering up phase is completed.

Ship Restrictions: linking and activation may only be performed by Carriers.		 Mobile Analysis Beacon

92514 - Ultratidal Entropic Disintegrator II This extra-large Entropic Disintegrator is only seen in use on Triglavian capital ships, these massive ships being capable of managing the considerable radiation and enormous gravitational tidal forces the weapon generates. At the energy levels of this ultraheavy weapon system, the tidal forces are so powerful that even the special systems built into battleships are insufficient and only capital ships can deal with the forces involved.

Entropic Disintegrators draw on the tremendous power of the Triglavian singularity-based energy systems to convert exotic matter into a particle stream directed with locally generated entropic force. While powerful, the range of the weapon is limited by the attenuation of entropic forces, which dissipate critically beyond the optimal range. As a result this weapon has no falloff range.

The particle stream generates thermal and explosive reactions on impact, and the entropic forces resolve into a localized gravitational conduit that steadily increases the acceleration on the exotic particles. In effect, the weapon's damage potential increases to a maximum level as long as the particle stream is kept on the same target.

Requires exotic plasma charge ammo types: Baryon, Meson, and Tetryon.		 Precursor Weapon

92661 - Cheetah Zydrine Burn SKIN Zydrine Burn is a potent liquor that is loosely related to the more refined Zydrine Wine, both of these green-hued drinks being produced using rice leaves, a certain portion of the grains, and whatever additives are appropriate to the style of drink. While Zydrine Wine can be an extraordinarily delicate and subtle drink, with the finest generally held to be brewed from the rice plants of Intaki Prime, its more powerful cousin is a somewhat pungent and vividly green brew. Rumors suggest that some versions of Zydrine Burn use as ingredients effluent from Quafe production, liquefied fedo scent glands, or even the notorious protein delicacies in powdered form. Whatever the case, a market for this harshly memorable liquor has sprung up among space workers of all kinds, and few space station bars lack a bottle or two of the stuff. Among planetary populations the brew has a more notorious reputation, popularly considered the tipple of underclasses, criminals, and ruthless capsuleer pirates. Permanent SKIN

92958 - Gallente Election Expert System <font size="14">Gallente Election Expert System </font>

This Expert System makes available skills enabling a capsuleer to fly Gallente Tech 1 and Navy frigate-type, destroyer-type and cruiser-type ships along with Gallente-focused supporting skills. This is a promotional Expert System released to celebrate the Federation Day.

The temporary skills provided by this Expert System last for four days.

An Expert System is a remote, restricted artificial intelligence providing you with access to certain skills during the active rental period. As it is independent from your clone and your capsule, an active Expert System is not lost on pod death or clone jump.

<font size="14">Activating an Expert System</font>

Activation of an Expert System is automatic upon redemption of the item by the specific capsuleer intending to use the service.

Expert Systems are a product developed by the PKN Interstellar consortium, made available over the HyperNet FTL communications network, and marketed by PKN Interstellar member corporations. An Expert System is a restricted AI based on artificial gelbrain technology. As the Expert System uses neural pathways based on those created by skill training or skill injection, it is compatible with capsule-ship interface and control systems. Real time command and control communication is achieved using dedicated FTL channels on PKN Interstellar's HyperNet.		 Promotional Expert Systems

1037134 Ultratidal Entropic Disintegrator II Ultratidal Entropic Disintegrator II Name of item 92514 (Precursor Weapon)
1037135 This extra-large Entropic Disintegrator is only seen in use on Triglavian capital ships, these massive ships being capable of managing the considerable radiation and enormous gravitational tidal forces the weapon generates. At the energy levels of this ultraheavy weapon system, the tidal forces are so powerful that even the special systems built into battleships are insufficient and only capital ships can deal with the forces involved.

Entropic Disintegrators draw on the tremendous power of the Triglavian singularity-based energy systems to convert exotic matter into a particle stream directed with locally generated entropic force. While powerful, the range of the weapon is limited by the attenuation of entropic forces, which dissipate critically beyond the optimal range. As a result this weapon has no falloff range.

The particle stream generates thermal and explosive reactions on impact, and the entropic forces resolve into a localized gravitational conduit that steadily increases the acceleration on the exotic particles. In effect, the weapon's damage potential increases to a maximum level as long as the particle stream is kept on the same target.

Requires exotic plasma charge ammo types: Baryon, Meson, and Tetryon. 1037608 This device contains a nanobot swarm (or nanoswarm), suspended within a solution. They were created to support the Fabricator in its manufacturing processes.

Once primed for use, the device can be destroyed, unleashing the nanoswarm on the surrounding environment, where they will apply a specific effect. If another device is destroyed first, or they are allowed to expire, the nanoswarm will become inert.		 This device contains a nanobot swarm (or nanoswarm), suspended within a solution. 1037675 Ultratidal Entropic Disintegrator II Blueprint Ultratidal Entropic Disintegrator II Blueprint Name of item 92654 (Precursor Weapon Blueprint)
1037699 Zydrine Burn is a potent liquor that is loosely related to the more refined Zydrine Wine, both of these green-hued drinks being produced using rice leaves, a certain portion of the grains, and whatever additives are appropriate to the style of drink. While Zydrine Wine can be an extraordinarily delicate and subtle drink, with the finest generally held to be brewed from the rice plants of Intaki Prime, its more powerful cousin is a somewhat pungent and vividly green brew. Rumors suggest that some versions of Zydrine Burn use as ingredients effluent from Quafe production, liquefied fedo scent glands, or even the notorious protein delicacies in powdered form. Whatever the case, a market for this harshly memorable liquor has sprung up among space workers of all kinds, and few space station bars lack a bottle or two of the stuff. Among planetary populations the brew has a more notorious reputation, popularly considered the tipple of underclasses, criminals, and ruthless capsuleer pirates. Among planetary populations the brew has a more notorious reputation, popularly considered the tipple of underclasses, criminals, and ruthless capsuleer pirates. Zydrine Burn is a potent liquor that is loosely related to the more refined Zydrine Wine, both of these green-hued drinks being produced using rice leaves, a certain portion of the grains, and whatever additives are appropriate to the style of drink. While Zydrine Wine can be an extraordinarily delicate and subtle drink, with the finest generally held to be brewed from the rice plants of Intaki Prime, its more powerful cousin is a somewhat pungent and vividly green brew. Rumors suggest that some versions of Zydrine Burn use as ingredients effluent from Quafe production, liquefied fedo scent glands, or even the notorious protein delicacies in powdered form. Whatever the case, a market for this harshly memorable liquor has sprung up among space workers of all kinds, and few space station bars lack a bottle or two of the stuff. Among planetary populations the brew has a more notorious reputation, popularly considered the tipple of underclasses, criminals, and ruthless capsuleer pirates. 1038742 <font size="14">Gallente Election Expert System </font>

This Expert System makes available skills enabling a capsuleer to fly Gallente Tech 1 and Navy frigate-type, destroyer-type and cruiser-type ships along with Gallente-focused supporting skills. This is a promotional Expert System released to celebrate the Federation Day.

The temporary skills provided by this Expert System last for four days.

An Expert System is a remote, restricted artificial intelligence providing you with access to certain skills during the active rental period. As it is independent from your clone and your capsule, an active Expert System is not lost on pod death or clone jump.

<font size="14">Activating an Expert System</font>

Activation of an Expert System is automatic upon redemption of the item by the specific capsuleer intending to use the service.

Expert Systems are a product developed by the PKN Interstellar consortium, made available over the HyperNet FTL communications network, and marketed by PKN Interstellar member corporations. An Expert System is a restricted AI based on artificial gelbrain technology. As the Expert System uses neural pathways based on those created by skill training or skill injection, it is compatible with capsule-ship interface and control systems. Real time command and control communication is achieved using dedicated FTL channels on PKN Interstellar's HyperNet.		 <font size="14"><b>Gallente Election Expert System </b></font>
